name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:2 Twin Beds Standard 
info:Stayed in July 2023
info:Family
info:6 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted July 16, 2023
msg:The second stop in Hefei wanted to live in the old city and feel the fireworks of this thousand-year-old city, so I chose this hotel.

Location traffic:
The location is quite good. Shuanggang Old Street, Gongchen Street, and Xiaoyaojin Park are all nearby. There are all kinds of snacks around, and they are all old shops that have been open for many years. If it is not popular, the pedestrian street and Evergrande Night Market are also within walking distance. The only downside is that there is no subway nearby.

Serve:
The service is worse than the average five-star hotel, but better than Express.
Room facilities:
The gate is the standard Crowne Plaza style, the one with a gate head, very grand. Although the decoration of the lobby is a bit old, the design is good and the grade is still very high. It's different as soon as you enter the room. The room is very small and far from the usual standard of Crowne Plaza. The decoration of the room is very simple, it is the style of express hotel, and it is very old. The sanitation is fairly clean, but the room is damp and there are mosquitoes in the room. There is no bathtub in the room, other facilities are also very simple, and the spare parts are only at the level of express hotels, and the bathrobes and towels are very old.

swimming pool:
The swimming pool is relatively large and the facilities are okay. Many children learn to swim here, and the water temperature is around 28¬∞C. But the facilities in the shower area are very old and some facilities are broken. Slippers were scattered all over the floor.

The location of this hotel is excellent, the facilities are average, although the price is cheap, but the price/performance ratio is not high, and the same price is far lower than that of local brand hotels. Although it is a Crowne Plaza brand, it is also a Crowne Plaza Express Hotel.
